	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '04845f79b9bb39810f99c270d4ce02c87f25705b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '04845f79b9bb39810f99c270d4ce02c87f25705b') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'fd80c904b53c5a538473f873f6ca8534cd6df060') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '04845f79b9bb39810f99c270d4ce02c87f25705b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') != '94ad0108fc95790a2752bd27752b595a4c60e508') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== '94ad0108fc95790a2752bd27752b595a4c60e508') {

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '8b9b61de833bcfa7fdab936b084062e4f4660eb9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '8b9b61de833bcfa7fdab936b084062e4f4660eb9') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'ab6947edca8eba33260c79a4e501dfc239575d0c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '8b9b61de833bcfa7fdab936b084062e4f4660eb9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') != '754498d9f145fcd64f5a24cf69c5e132deed6127') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '754498d9f145fcd64f5a24cf69c5e132deed6127') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');

			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_28();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '754498d9f145fcd64f5a24cf69c5e132deed6127') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html');
	writefile_29();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html') != '0798e6e6f315d5125067e82cea25cb9a21c5ffea') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html') !== '0798e6e6f315d5125067e82cea25cb9a21c5ffea') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html') !== 'd0f18a7fe7dd05665102db628b6cc6f028240e0b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_29();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html') !== '0798e6e6f315d5125067e82cea25cb9a21c5ffea') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/setup.part.html');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') != 'cd325e937b7dddf27fa0f1df50d7322e3e004fde') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== 'cd325e937b7dddf27fa0f1df50d7322e3e004fde') {

			if (!@copy('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');

			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_34();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== 'e8a1149a7f26117e0b69832d6de869f45dd37fe1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}

	writefile_39();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php') != '5d59b9bf4384f0b905abd22cef614e3895dd9a0d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php') !== '5d59b9bf4384f0b905abd22cef614e3895dd9a0d') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php');

			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_39();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php') !== '5d59b9bf4384f0b905abd22cef614e3895dd9a0d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php');
